CREATE TABLE cuentas (
	idcuenta bigserial NOT NULL,
	codcue varchar(35) NOT NULL,
	nomcue varchar(60) NOT NULL,
	movcue bool NOT NULL,
	idnivel int2 NOT NULL,
	grucue varchar(30) NOT NULL,
	asodebe varchar(35) NULL,
	asohaber varchar(35) NULL,
	tiptran int2 DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
	sigef bool NOT NULL,
	grubalances int4 NULL,
	grufluefec int4 NULL,
	resulcostos int2 NULL,
	balancostos int2 NULL,
	usucrea int4 NOT NULL,
	feccrea timestamp NOT NULL,
	usumodi int4 NULL,
	fecmodi timestamp NULL,
	CONSTRAINT cuentas_pk PRIMARY KEY (idcuenta)
);
